Battle for Zendikar RPTQ Edmonton
=================================



 Posted in [ARCHIVES](/en/articles/archive)
 on July 10, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast










* [Pro Tour *Battle for Zendikar* Regional Pro Tour Qualifier Top 8 Decklists](http://magic.wizards.com/en/articles/archive/organized-play/the-pro-tour-main-stage-2015-07-10)


Thanks to [Warp 2 Comics & Games](http://www.warpcomics.com/) for organizing this Regional Pro Tour Qualifier and submitting Top 8 decklists!
